The basic room should be around 700 rmb and if you are going to keep that price point with the minibar give more options.

posted:Posted July 18, 2023
msg:Because I had a good impression of staying during the epidemic last year, of course I chose to come back when I came to Beijing for the first time this year, and I chose a larger room type. Unfortunately, the check-in experience was very uncomfortable. Although the room is 10 square meters larger, the layout is not very reasonable, and the space is wasted. For example, the space by the window facing the head of the bed is simply empty, and the ambient light tubes are not even laid, which seems strange; the shower room is too long and empty, There is no table to sit on, and the comfort is not enough; there is a bathtub next to the bed in the room, but it is a few centimeters above the room level, and there are steps, which may pose a safety hazard. The washbasin didn't drain well and needed to be unplugged. The most disappointing thing is the hotel's parking. First of all, the location is not good. The underground parking lot is located on the ground floor of the opposite commercial building. You need to take the elevator of the commercial building to the ground floor and go back to the hotel across the street instead of the elevator directly to the hotel. The lobby; the second is the service. I stayed for three nights. On the second night, a friend came to visit and talked until late at night. I called to inquire about picking up the car. The answer was that the guard would accompany me to the ba*****t to pick up the car, which made me feel at ease. , Because my friend is a single lady, I was a little worried about safety when I walked to the underground garage of the opposite building late at night. But I didn't expect the on-site operation to be: the doorman asked a lady to go to the ba*****t to pick up the car by herself, pay at the exit, and then walk to the doorman to ask him for reimbur*****t? My friend didn't care about it, and left after following the guard's instructions. When he visited the next day, he told me that my jaw dropped in shock! This level of service does not match the hotel's high-end positioning, glamorous appearance and room rates!
